        disable         = yes
        type            = INTERNAL UNLISTED
        id              = daytime-dgram
        socket_type     = dgram
        protocol        = udp
        user            = root
        wait            = yes
        port            = 13
}                                                                               
service echo
{
        type            = INTERNAL
        id              = echo-stream
        socket_type     = stream
        protocol        = tcp
        user            = root
        wait            = no
        disable         = yes
}                                                                               
service echo
{
        type            = INTERNAL UNLISTED
        id              = echo-dgram
        socket_type     = dgram
        protocol        = udp
        user            = root
        wait            = yes
        disable         = yes
        port            = 7
}                                                                               
service seosload
{
        flags                   = REUSE IPv6
        disable = no
        socket_type             = stream
        wait                    = no
        user                    = root
        log_on_success          += USERID
        log_on_failure          += USERID
        server                  = /apps/opt/seos/lbin/rseloadd
}
service rsync
{
        disable = yes
        socket_type     = stream
        wait            = no
        user            = root
        server          = /usr/bin/rsync
        server_args     = --daemon
        log_on_failure  += USERID
}
service time
{
        type            = INTERNAL
        id              = time-stream
        socket_type     = stream
        protocol        = tcp
        user            = root
        wait            = no
        disable         = yes
}

{
        type            = INTERNAL UNLISTED
        id              = time-dgram
        socket_type     = dgram
        protocol        = udp
        user            = root
        wait            = yes
        disable         = yes
        port            = 37
}                                                                               
service vnetd
{
        socket_type             = stream
        protocol                = tcp
        wait                    = no
        user                    = root
        server                  = /usr/openv/bin/vnetd
        disable                 = no
        instances               = UNLIMITED
        cps                     = 1000 1
}

        disable                 = no
}

multiple programs on the system. In order to save disk space and
memory, as well as to make upgrading easier, common system code is
kept in one place and shared between programs. This particular package
contains the most important sets of shared libraries: the standard C

# can in this file.  \# comments out the line as in most shell commands.

DEBUG_SSI_NAV=${DEBUG_SSI_NAV:=not_set_or_null}
if [ "$DEBUG_SSI_NAV" != 'not_set_or_null' ] ; then set -x ; fi
get_host_values() {
        if [ "$DEBUG_SSI_NAV" != 'not_set_or_null' ] ; then set -x ; fi
        if [ "${SSI_STATUS}" = "" ]
        then    if [ -f "${SSIHOSTFILE}" ]
                then
                        SSI_INTEGRITY=Host_File_Syntax_Error:${SSIHOSTFILE}
                        . ${SSIHOSTFILE}
                else
                        echo "$0: cannot locate SSI host file: ${SSIHOSTFILE}" >&2
                        SSI_STATUS=Fail
                fi
        fi
} # end of get_host_values()
get_site_values() {
        if [ "$DEBUG_SSI_NAV" != 'not_set_or_null' ] ; then set -x ; fi
        # can't get here unless ${HOST_SITE_NAME} was non-null!
        export SSISITEFILE
        SSISITEFILE=${SSIDIR}/site.${HOST_SITE_NAME}
        if [ "${SSI_STATUS}" = "" ]
        then    if [ -f "${SSISITEFILE}" ]
                then
                        SSI_INTEGRITY=Site_File_Syntax_Error:${SSISITEFILE}
                        . ${SSISITEFILE}
                else
                        echo "$0: cannot locate SSI site file: ${SSISITEFILE}" >&2
                        SSI_STATUS=Fail
                fi
        fi
} # end of get_site_values()
read_in_the_ssi_files() {
        if [ "$DEBUG_SSI_NAV" != 'not_set_or_null' ] ; then set -x ; fi
        if [ -d "${Anchor}" ]
        then
                export SSIDIR
                SSIDIR=${Anchor}/etc/SSI
                if [ -d "${SSIDIR}" ]
                then
                        export SSIHOSTFILE
                        SSIHOSTFILE=${SSIDIR}/host.ssi
                        get_host_values         # function that dots in host.ssi's values
                        if [ -n "$HOST_SITE_NAME" ]     # if variable has a non-null value
                        then
                                get_site_values # function that dots in site.$HOST_SITE_NAME
                                get_host_values # reread host file to override site file's
                        fi
                else
                        echo "$0: cannot locate SSI directory: ${SSIDIR}" >&2
                        SSI_STATUS=Fail
                fi
        else
                echo "$0: cannot locate dir. $Anchor" >&2
                SSI_STATUS=Fail
        fi
} # end of read_in_the_ssi_files()
report_usage() {
        #echo "$USAGE_ssi_nav"
        grep '^# USAGE #' $0  | sed 's/^# USAGE #//'
} # end of report_usage()
SSI_INTEGRITY=Syntax_Error      # will be reassigned to indicate SSI file being sourced
SSI_STATUS=                     # remains null until/unless an error is found.
OUTPUT_USAGE_SSI_NAV=F          # remains 'F' unless -h or -? option is used.
ARG_1=${1:-null}                # use this to get around /sbin/sh error on HP-UX!
case "$ARG_1" in
-h|-\? ) OUTPUT_USAGE_SSI_NAV=T ;;
esac
if [ "$OUTPUT_USAGE_SSI_NAV" = 'T' ]
then
        report_usage
else
        case "`uname -s`" in
        HP-UX ) Anchor=${Anchor:=null_or_not_set}
                if [ "$Anchor" != 'null_or_not_set' ]
                then
                        if [ "${SSI_STATUS}" = "" ]
                        then    read_in_the_ssi_files
                        fi
                else
                        Anchor=`cat /etc/default/Loc_Env_Anchor 2>/dev/null`
                        if [ -n "${Anchor}" ]
                        then
                                if [ "${SSI_STATUS}" = "" ]
                                then    read_in_the_ssi_files
                                fi
                        else
                                echo "$0: cannot set Anchor! Does /etc/default/Loc_Env_Anchor exist? Are contents right?" >&2
                                SSI_STATUS=Fail
                        fi
                fi
                ;;
        * )     if [ -n "${Anchor}" ]   # not zero-length string; i.e., has a value
                then
                        if [ "${SSI_STATUS}" = "" ]
                        then    read_in_the_ssi_files
                        fi
                else
                        Anchor=`cat /etc/default/Loc_Env_Anchor 2>/dev/null`
                        if [ -n "${Anchor}" ]
                        then
                                if [ "${SSI_STATUS}" = "" ]
                                then    read_in_the_ssi_files
                                fi
                        else
                                echo "$0: cannot set Anchor! Does /etc/default/Loc_Env_Anchor exist? Are contents right?" >&2
                                SSI_STATUS=Fail
                        fi
                fi
                ;;
        esac
fi
if [ "${SSI_STATUS}" = "" ]
then    SSI_INTEGRITY=Pass
else    SSI_INTEGRITY="${SSI_STATUS}"
fi
unset SSI_STATUS USAGE_ssi_nav SSIDIR SSISITEFILE SSIHOSTFILE OUTPUT_USAGE_SSI_NAV ARG_1
if [ "$DEBUG_SSI_NAV" = 'not_set_or_null' ]
then                            # because during this script ...
        unset DEBUG_SSI_NAV     #    DEBUG_SSI_NAV=${DEBUG_SSI_NAV:=not_set_or_null}
else
        set +x                  #    -x was turned on because DEBUG_SSI_NAV had value
                                #    +x turns it (tracing) off.
fi
